 sansad ne aadhaar ke jariye kalyaan yojanaon kaa laabh labhaarthiyon tak sidhe pahunchane vaale aadhaar vidheyak ko manjuuri de di
 In this bill placed as a money bill by the government, the Rajya Sabha returned the Lok Sabha with five amendments, although the lower house rejected these amendments
 isse pehle loksabhaa aadhaar (vittiya or anya sahayikiyon, prasuvidhaon or sevaaon kaa lakshith paridaan) vidheyak 2016 ko shuukravaar ko paarit kar chuki thi
 In the Rajya Sabha, where the ruling NDA is in minority, the Bill was discussed today
 vidheyak par congress sahit vipaksh kii ore se paanch sanshodhan pesh kiye gaye jise ucch sadan ne sweekaar karke loksabhaa ko waapas bhej diya
 Shortly thereafter, the government brought the bill back to the Lok Sabha and Finance Minister Arun Jaitley, under pressure from the opposition in the upper house, urged the lower house to reject the amendments ranging from one to five as fatal, which the House Approved by voice
 rajyasabha main vipaksh ne in sanshodhano main rashtriya suraksha kii jagah saarvajanik apaat sthiti or saarvajanik suraksha shabdon ko samahit karne sahit mat vibhaajan ke jariye paanch sanshodhan vidheyak main samahit karaaye the
 The obligation to accept Aadhaar was also removed in these amendments
 isamen yah bhi samahit kiya gaya tha ki kisi vyakti ke bare main jaankaree saajha karne kii jaankaree dene vaale panel main sieji, sivisi ko bhi shaamil kiya jaae
 In the Lok Sabha, Jaitley said on these amendments that there were no such provisions in the similar bill brought by the UPA in 2010 and now the Congress is emphasizing these things and is creating complex idioms like public order, public safety, public emergency, the definition of which Is elaborate and may be misused
 unhone kaha ki lok suraksha or saarvajanik apaat sthiti to kahin kanoon vyavastha kii sthiti banane yaa kahin koi aapadaa aane par bhi kisi vyakti kii jaankaree kaa durupyog ho saktaa he
 No member of Congress was present in the House when this Bill came to Lok Sabha
 jetali ne is vidhyek ko dhan vidheyak ke rup main laane kii vipaksh kii aalochanaon ko khaarij karte hue kaha ki is vidheyak kaa makasad sabsidi ke jariye sarkaar dwaara pradutt raashi ko uske sahi hakdaaron tak pahunchaana he
 Just because the government order has been challenged and the matter is pending in the Supreme Court, the Parliament's right to make laws cannot be postponed
 ullekhneey he ki sarkaar agar ise dhan vidheyak ke rup main nahin laai hoti tab ucch sadan dwaara naamanzoor kiye jane par vah ise aage nahin badha paati
 The Finance Minister said that it is different from that old bill because it has made the provisions of data privacy related to people very strict
 unhone kaha ki upie ke anubhavon se sikh lete hue hamane gopneeyata ke praavdhaanon ko sakht banaaya he
 Only when there is a matter related to national security can a person's data be shared
 rajyasabha main kai sadasyon ne is vidheyak ke kanoon banane kii sthiti main niztaa kii suraksha ko lekar chintaa jataayi
 Jaitley said that biometric data can be shared only in the matter related to national security
 aankade saajha karne kaa faisla sanyukt sachiv rank se upar ke adhikari kar sakenge or cabinet sachiv kii adhyakshata vaali ek samiti isaki samiksha karegi
 Amid Tokatoki's discussion in the Rajya Sabha, Jaitley accused Jairam Ramesh of Congress of disrupting the path of a bill that was originally conceived by the UPA government
 jetali ne kaha ki rashtriya suraksha samvidhan main paribhaashit shabd he jiske apane myne hai or rashtriya suraksha ke sambandh main vyavhaarik hone par hi kuch jaankaree saajha kii ja sakati he
 The comments unhone kaha ki alpiji kaa maamla ek udhaaharan he ki jab isamen pratyaksh nakad antar kii vyavastha jodi gai thi tab kisi kisi ghar main 20-20 gas conection the or sarkaar kii sabsidi kaa paisa, un logon ko mil rahaa tha jo iske hakdaar nahin the
 In the case of gas connections, we have ensured to remove the rich people from the ambit of subsidy and bring the poor under its purview

 iske kuch hi der baad sarkaar is vidheyak ko loksabhaa main waapas lekar ai or vitt mantri arun jetali ne ucch sadan main vipaksh ke dabaav main ek se lekar paanch tak ke sanshodhano ko ghaatak bataate hue unhen asweekaar karne kaa nichle sadan se aagrah kiya jise sadan ne dhvanimat se manjuuri de di
 In the Rajya Sabha, the opposition had introduced five amendment bills through the division of votes including public emergency and public safety in place of national security in these amendments
 in sanshodhan main aadhaar ko sweekaar karne kii baadhyataa ko bhi hataa diya gaya tha
 It was also included that CAG, CVC should also be included in the panel for sharing information about a person
 loksabhaa main jetali ne in sanshodhano par kaha ki 2010 main upie dwaara laaye gaye aise hi vidheyak main ye praavdhaan nahin the or ab congress inhen chizon par jor de rahi he tathaa lok vyavastha, lok suraksha, saarvajanik apaat sthiti jaisi jatil muhaavarey garh rahi hajiski paribhaasha vistrut he or iskaa galat istemaal ho saktaa he
 He said that information of a person can be misused even if there is a situation of law and order or there is a disaster in public safety and public emergency
 is vidheyak ke loksabhaa main aane par sadan main congress kaa koi sadsy maujuud nahin tha
 Jaitley dismissed the opposition's criticisms of bringing this bill in the form of a money bill and said that the purpose of this bill is to transfer the amount paid by the government to its rightful holders through subsidy
 keval isliye ki sarkari aadesh ko chunauti di gai or maamla ucchtam nyaayalay main lambit he, isliye kanoon banane ke sansad ke adhikaar ko sthagit nahin kiya ja saktaa
 It is worth mentioning that if the government had not brought it in the form of a money bill, then it would not have been able to take it forward if it was rejected by the Upper House
 vitt mantri ne kaha ki yah us puraane vidheyak se bhinn he kyonki isamen logon se jude aankadon kii gopneeyata ke praavdhaanon ko kaaphi sakht banaaya gaya he
 He said that learning from the experiences of the UPA, we have tightened the privacy provisions
 sirf rashtriya suraksha se jude maamla hone par hi kisi vyakti ke aankade saajha kiye ja sakenge
 Many members in the Rajya Sabha raised concerns about privacy protection in the event of the bill becoming law
 jetali ne kaha ki rashtriya suraksha se jude maamle main hi biomitric aankade saajha kiye ja sakate hai
 Officers above the rank of Joint Secretary will be able to decide the data sharing and a committee headed by Cabinet Secretary will review it
 rajyasabha main charchaa ke dauraan tokaatoki ke bich jetali ne congress ke jairam ramesh par aarope lagaaya ki vah aise vidheyak kii raah main vyavdhaan daal rahe hai jo mul rup se upie sarkaar kii pariklpana tha
 Jaitley said that national security is a term defined in the constitution which has its own meaning and some information can be shared only when it is practical in relation to national security
 tippaniyan He said that the case of LPG is an example that when a direct cash gap was added to it, then there were 20 to 20 gas connections in a house and the government was getting subsidy money to those who were not entitled to it
